 K
 prasad ne haal hi main team india ke purv captain mahendra singh dhoni ke bhavishya ko lekar sawaal uthaae the
 But the team's head coach Ravi Shastri differs from Prasad
 shastri ne dhoni ke paksh main bayaan dete hue kaha ki unke maujuuda form ko dekhte hue team prabandhan unhen team se hataane ke bare main soch bhi nahin saktaa
 Dhoni showed tremendous form on the tour of Sri Lanka 82
 23 strike rate se 162 ran banaae the saath hi wicket ke peeche bhi gajab kii chapaltaa dikhaai
 Dhoni also became the first wicketkeeper to perform 100 stumpings in odis on this tour
 ravi shastri ne ek nijee channel se baatcheet main kaha ki dhoni ke sathfitness or formdonon hai or team ko 2019 vishwa cap main unki jarurat hogi
 Shastri compared Dhoni with legendary batsmen Sunil Gavaskar, Sachin Tendulkar and all-rounder Kapil Dev, saying that it is necessary to honor his achievements
 shastri ne kaha, " dhoni jaisaa lijend aapako kahaan milegaa? dhoni sunil gavaskar, sachin tendulkar or kapil dev ke baraabar hai
 We should honor his achievements
 " shastri ne srilanka main dhoni ke pradarshan kii tarif karte hue kaha ki unamem abhi bahut cricket baaki he
 Shastri said, "A player is evaluated on the basis of his current form and fitness and Dhoni has these two
 agar aap unki wicketcaping dekhen to vanade cricket main vah sarvshereshth hai
 His fitness is amazing, he batted very well in Sri Lanka and let me tell you that what you saw in Sri Lanka was just a trailer
 ab film kaa intjaar kiijie
 "shastri said," If Dhoni keeps playing like this, then there is no reason why he will not be in the team for the 2019 World Cup
 aap dhoni ke bagaiyr team kii kalpana hi nahin kar sakate
 On the question of not keeping Yuvraj Singh and Suresh Raina in the team, Shastri said, "the doors are not locked
 feet hone par hi team main shaamil kiya jayega
 "shastri said that he has spoken to the BCCI about resting the players after the series against Australia
 unhone kaha, "behatar hota ki tii-20 baad main karavaate kyonki srilanka siries or dakshin africa ke daure ke bich bahut kam samay hoga
 He said that the first two matches of the five-match ODI series against Australia would be important
 shastri ne kaha, "hamen donon match jeetne honge kyonki pehle do match hi siries kaa faisla kar denge
 Australia will give a tough challenge
 "shastri ne kaha, "ye dekhne ke liye shaayad main jinda na rahun ki jis tarah hamaari team ne srilanka main sabhi match jite usee tarah australia yaa phir england main bhi jite
 "shastri clarified that he had no role in the selection of the team
 unhone kaha, "main chayan main dakhal nahin detaa hum, jo team milegi usko taiyaar karuunga
 " haal hi main film 'singh ij bling' main apane ection or stant se darshakon ko hairaan karne vaali emi jackson film main apane kirdaar ke liye khub saraahna bator rahi hai
 Amy Jackson, who is a hit, shared many experiences related to her film 'singh is Bling'
 emi ke saath hui baatcheet ke pesh hai kuch khaas ansh:pehali baar aisa hua he kii akshay kumaar kifilmaki actress kii bhi zyada charchaa ho rahi he?sabase pehle main akshay kaa shukriya kahana chaahati hum ki unhone mujhe film main sab kuch karne kaa mauka diya
 i enjoyed every moment
 akshay kumarkhud ek ection star hai lekin unhone mujhe bhi ection karne diya, ye unka badppan he
 Are you aware of Indian films and songs? Yes, recently we went to a function and there was a song 'dheer Dheere Se', which was from the original Aashiqui, we were very happy to hear
 aapane'singh ij bling'main ection kiya he kya aane vaale dinon main solo filmein bhi karengi jo ection par aadhaarit hongi?main jarur karnaa chaahuungi, jaisi 'kil bill' film wo bhi bhartiya style main
 People have accepted the action
 main jarur karnaa chaahuungi
 Someone approached you for an action film? Yes, a big announcement could be made soon this week
 uske bare main zyada baat nahin kar sakati
 It is not completely but yes there will be a lot of action in the film
 film'singh ij bling'kaa pasandida seen koun sa tha?jab bhi lara datta or akshay kumaar screen par hote the, mujhe wo seen kaaphi dilachasp lagate the
 Did you say that you want to work with Salman Khan? Yes, unfortunately a few years ago i was not able to be a part of 'kick' with Salman Khan because South's film was in contract with i (I)
 lekin main jarur karnaa chaahuungi
 i wanted to work with Akshay and Salman before doing films
 saal 2015 aapke liye khaas rahaa?shat pratishat khaas saal rahaa
 i finished 3 films this year
 dhanush ke saath-south kii or 'singh ij bling' ke alaava ek or south kii film kii he
 Dhanush's film will be released on Diwali
 or jald hi main south main 'vijay' ke saath kaam karne vaali hum
 Bollywood is my priority but i will also continue to do South films
 south ke superstar 'vijay' ke saath koun si film he?main chote baalo main ek skool teacher ke kirdaar main hum
 Is a very different character
 dhanush ke saath bhi aap kai filmein kar rahi hai, anubhav kaisaa rahaa?maine bahut kuch unase siikhaa he

 yah tivi technology main ek nayaa industry benchmark he or ise lakjri gharon ko ghayan main rakhkar utaara gaya he
 The highlight of the TV is its 8K resolution, 8K AI upscaling, quantum processor 8K and quantum HDR, all of which together give the Stunning 8K experience
 Samsung QLED 8K TV ke chaar model hai- 98 inch, 82 inch, 75 inch or 65 inch jo 33 million picksal ke saath aate hai, 4K uechdi tivi ke chaar guna or phul echdi tivi ke 16 guna
 The 75 inch model of Samsung QLED 8K TV is priced at Rs 10,99,900, the 82 inch model is priced at Rs 16,99,900, the 98 inch model is priced at Rs 59,99,900
 philhal, iskaa keval 98 inch model hi order karne ke liye uplabdh karaayaa jayega, jabaki 65 inch (july main kharidne ke liye uplabdh) model kii keemat kii ghoshnaa jald kii jaaegi
 One of the key features of the new TV is the quantum processor 8K, which will ensure that users are viewing content through HDMI, USB or any set-top box, rather than content native resolution at 8K resolution
 yah is tivi kii ek badi khubi he, jaisaa ki ham sabhi jaanate hai ki hamaare paas zyada 8K content uplabdh nahin he lekin tivi content ke original rijolution ke bajaay 8ke rijolution main content ko dikhayega
 The new tvs come with voice commands
 tivi main Bixby 2
 0 and Google Assistant support will also be available
 Samsung brands ke ye letest tivi for field wais capability feechar se las he, is feechar kii madad se wais cmand ke liye tivi remote aapke paas ho aisa jaruri nahin he
 The new TV has Apple Airplay 2 support with the help of which users will be able to mirror and play content directly from their Apple device on Samsung QLED tvs
 QLED 8K range ke alaava samsung ne 2019 ke liye apane QLED TV linep ko bhi apadet kiya he

 nae jajon kii niyukti ke saath hi supreme court main jajon kii sankhya badhkar 34 ho gai he
 Among the new judges, Justice Ramasubramanian, Justice Krishna Murari, Justice s Ravindra Bhatt and Justice Hrishikesh Roy have been appointed by the President
 isse pehle supreme court main jajon kii sankhya 31 thi
 The Central Government had recently increased to 34, including the Chief Justice
 supreme court colegium ne himachal pradesh hai court ke chif justise ram subramanyan, punjab or haryana hai court ke justise krishna murari, rajasthan hai court ke aar ravindra bhatta or kerala hai court se hrishikesh roy ke naam kii sifarish sarkaar ko bheji thi
